Changelog

Date Author Change
2019-11-08 Denis Arnaud - 1.69.0-4 - Fixed the runtime dependency on python3-numpy

2019-01-23 Denis Arnaud - 1.69.0-1 - Transformed boost-1.69.0-1 into boost169-1.69.0-1 (BZ#1667725)
